
[grammar] 
	[nterm] 
		[program] 
			nullable	True
			first : basic
			follow : 
		[fundefs] 
			nullable	True
			first : basic
			follow : basic
		[fundef] 
			nullable	False
			first : basic
			follow : basic
		[F] 
			nullable	True
			first : 
			follow : (
		[iargs] 
			nullable	True
			first : basic
			follow : ), ,
		[block] 
			nullable	False
			first : {
			follow : basic
		[iarg] 
			nullable	False
			first : basic
			follow : ), ,
		[type] 
			nullable	False
			first : basic
			follow : id, [
		[decls] 
			nullable	True
			first : 
			follow : }, basic
		[stmts] 
			nullable	True
			first : 
			follow : }, id, if, while, do, return, {
		[decl] 
			nullable	False
			first : basic
			follow : }, basic
		[stmt] 
			nullable	False
			first : id, if, while, do, return, {
			follow : else, while, }, id, if, do, return, {
		[loc] 
			nullable	False
			first : id
			follow : =, [
		[bool] 
			nullable	False
			first : !, -, (, id, num, real, true, false
			follow : ;, ), ], or
		[M] 
			nullable	True
			first : 
			follow : id, if, while, do, return, {, ;
		[N] 
			nullable	True
			first : 
			follow : (, id, if, while, do, return, {
		[arg] 
			nullable	False
			first : id, !, -, (, num, real, true, false
			follow : ;
		[args] 
			nullable	True
			first : id, !, -, (, num, real, true, false
			follow : ,, )
		[join] 
			nullable	False
			first : !, -, (, id, num, real, true, false
			follow : and, ;, ), ], or
		[equality] 
			nullable	False
			first : !, -, (, id, num, real, true, false
			follow : eq, neq, and, ;, ), ], or
		[rel] 
			nullable	False
			first : !, -, (, id, num, real, true, false
			follow : <, <=, >=, >, eq, neq, and, ;, ), ], or
		[expr] 
			nullable	False
			first : !, -, (, id, num, real, true, false
			follow : +, -, <, <=, >=, >, eq, neq, and, ;, ), ], or
		[term] 
			nullable	False
			first : !, -, (, id, num, real, true, false
			follow : *, /, mod, +, -, <, <=, >=, >, eq, neq, and, ;, ), ], or
		[unary] 
			nullable	False
			first : !, -, (, id, num, real, true, false
			follow : *, /, mod, +, -, <, <=, >=, >, eq, neq, and, ;, ), ], or
		[factor] 
			nullable	False
			first : (, id, num, real, true, false
			follow : *, /, mod, +, -, <, <=, >=, >, eq, neq, and, ;, ), ], or
	[term] 
		$	0
		basic	1
		id	2
		(	3
		)	4
		,	5
		{	6
		}	7
		;	8
		[	9
		num	10
		]	11
		=	12
		if	13
		else	14
		while	15
		do	16
		return	17
		or	18
		and	19
		eq	20
		neq	21
		<	22
		<=	23
		>=	24
		>	25
		+	26
		-	27
		*	28
		/	29
		mod	30
		!	31
		real	32
		true	33
		false	34
	[rules] 
		0 : program, fundefs
		1 : fundefs, fundefs, fundef
		2 : fundefs, fundef
		3 : fundefs
		4 : fundef, basic, id, F, (, iargs, ), block
		5 : iargs, iargs, ,, iarg
		6 : iargs, iarg
		7 : iargs
		8 : iarg, type, id
		9 : block, {, decls, stmts, }
		10 : decls, decls, decl
		11 : decls
		12 : decl, type, id, ;
		13 : type, type, [, num, ]
		14 : type, basic
		15 : stmts, stmts, stmt
		16 : stmts
		17 : stmt, loc, =, bool, ;
		18 : stmt, if, (, bool, ), M, stmt
		19 : stmt, if, (, bool, ), M, stmt, else, M, stmt
		20 : stmt, while, N, (, bool, ), M, stmt
		21 : stmt, do, N, stmt, while, (, bool, ), M, ;
		22 : stmt, return, arg, ;
		23 : stmt, block
		24 : args, args, ,, arg
		25 : args, arg
		26 : args
		27 : M
		28 : N
		29 : F
		30 : loc, loc, [, bool, ]
		31 : loc, id
		32 : bool, bool, or, join
		33 : bool, join
		34 : join, join, and, equality
		35 : join, equality
		36 : equality, equality, eq, rel
		37 : equality, equality, neq, rel
		38 : equality, rel
		39 : rel, rel, <, expr
		40 : rel, rel, <=, expr
		41 : rel, rel, >=, expr
		42 : rel, rel, >, expr
		43 : rel, expr
		44 : expr, expr, +, term
		45 : expr, expr, -, term
		46 : expr, term
		47 : term, term, *, unary
		48 : term, term, /, unary
		49 : term, term, mod, unary
		50 : term, unary
		51 : unary, !, unary
		52 : unary, -, unary
		53 : unary, factor
		54 : factor, (, bool, )
		55 : factor, loc
		56 : factor, id, (, args, )
		57 : factor, num
		58 : factor, real
		59 : factor, true
		60 : factor, false
		61 : arg, loc
		62 : arg, bool
